## System Prompt

<details><summary>Prompt injected by maze-symphony</summary>

## Task

Implement the following GitHub Issue:

**prim/maze#120**: Python testdata 全量回归存在 7 个失败用例，需按版本兼容路径修复

## 背景

在最新 `master` 上顺序执行了 `testdata/python` 下全部可运行用例（共 16 个），当前结果为 9 个通过、7 个失败，说明 Python testdata 主线尚未全绿。

本次回归严格按照仓库约束执行：每个用例均通过 `python3 testdata/run_test.py <case>` 单独运行，未并行执行多个 testdata。

详细测试记录见：`dev-log/2026-03-12-python-testdata-regression-scan.md`

## 当前结果

### 通过用例（9）

- `python/20260128-basic`
- `python/20260129-complex-types-39`
- `python/20260129-complex-types-310`
- `python/20260129-complex-types-311`
- `python/20260129-complex-types-312`
- `python/20260131-complex-types-3000`
- `python/20260201-py-merge`
- `python/20260201-class-merge-py311`
- `python/20260211-comprehensive-types`

### 失败用例（7）

1. `python/20260129-complex-types`
   - `PersonClass` 校验失败，期望数量 `>= 100`，实际匹配异常

2. `python/20260129-complex-types-27`
   - `pymempool_objects = 24348`，低于阈值 `> 30000`

3. `python/20260129-complex-types-35`
   - `pymempool_objects = 26863`，低于阈值 `> 50000`

4. `python/20260129-complex-types-36`
   - `pymempool_objects = 34587`，低于阈值 `> 50000`

5. `python/20260129-complex-types-37`
   - `pymempool_objects` 已过阈值，但 `PersonClass not found`

6. `python/20260129-complex-types-38`
   - `deque` 计数偏差，期望 `300`，实际 `301`

7. `python/20260201-class-merge-py27`
   - `Inner dict {int => int}<256` 未找到
   - `Outer dict {\"a\", \"b\"}` 未出现在预期结果中

## 初步判断

失败分布显示：

- `py39+` 主线整体稳定
- `py27/35/36/37` 存在明显兼容性或类型识别回归
- `py38` 更像边界统计偏差
- `class-merge-py27` 与 `class-merge-py311` 差异明显，旧版本 class merge 路径需要专项检查

## 需要完成的工作

1. 复查 `complex-types` 系列在 Python 2.7 / 3.5 / 3.6 / 3.7 下的对象识别与 `pymempool_objects` 统计链路
2. 排查 `PersonClass` 在旧版本输出中的命名/分类/聚合逻辑差异
3. 判断 `python/20260129-complex-types-38` 的 `deque=301` 是真实统计波动还是 off-by-one 缺陷
4. 排查 `python/20260201-class-merge-py27` 的 inner/outer dict 丢失原因
5. 修复后重新执行全部 Python testdata，目标达到全量通过
6. 更新必要的测试断言或兼容性文档

## 验收标准

- `testdata/python` 下全部可运行用例顺序执行后全部通过
- 覆盖至少 `py27`、`py311`、`py312` 三类代表版本验证
- 修复后无新增 Python testdata 回归
- 失败根因与修复结果有 dev-log 记录

```
56: 	old := *pq
```

18: // 只检查 ob_type 和 ob_refcnt，不做完整验证
19: func IsPyObjectWeak(address, size uint64) (bool, uint64, uint64) {
20: 	pyt := PyTypeAddressSafe(address + sizeof_pygc_head)
21: 	if pyt == 0 {
22: 		return false, address, pyt
23: 	}
24: 	address += sizeof_pygc_head
25: 	ob_refcnt := Refcnt(address)
26: 	_, ok := PyTypeName[pyt]
27: 	return ok && (ob_refcnt >= 0 && ob_refcnt < 100*10000), address, pyt
28: }

18: // 只检查 ob_type 和 ob_refcnt，不做完整验证
19: func IsPyObjectWeak(address, size uint64) (bool, uint64, uint64) {
20: 	pyt := PyTypeAddressSafe(address + sizeof_pygc_head)
21: 	if pyt == 0 {
22: 		return false, address, pyt
23: 	}

25: 	ob_refcnt := Refcnt(address)

13: func classifyMethodObject(pyo, pyt, realSize, merge uint64, sizeOfNode *ClassifyNodeSizeOfTree) (uint64, uint64, bool) {
14: 	function := pyMethodObject(pyo).Im_func()
15: 	code := pyFunctionObject(function).Func_code()
16: 	ct := LambdaTypePool.Get().(*ClassifyLambdaType)
17: 	ct.Type = LambdaType_Method
18: 	ct.Code = code
19: 	class := ct.T()
20: 	LambdaTypePool.Put(ct)
21: 	return class, realSize, true
22: }
23: 
24: func classifyFunctionObject(pyo, pyt, realSize, merge uint64, sizeOfNode *ClassifyNodeSizeOfTree) (uint64, uint64, bool) {
25: 	class, sizeof, addToObjects := classifyOtherObject(pyo, pyt, realSize, merge, sizeOfNode)
26: 	code := pyFunctionObject(pyo).Func_code()
27: 	funcName := GetCachedCstr(pyCodeObject(code).Co_name())
28: 	if funcName == "<lambda>" {
29: 		ct := LambdaTypePool.Get().(*ClassifyLambdaType)
30: 		ct.Type = LambdaType_Lambda
31: 		ct.Code = code
32: 		class = ct.T()
33: 		LambdaTypePool.Put(ct)
34: 	}

### `04:38:11` Step 34

---
## Goal

Implement GitHub issue `prim/maze#120`: fix Python testdata regressions so that all runnable cases under `testdata/python` pass when executed sequentially via the real acceptance path:

```bash
python3 testdata/run_test.py <case>
```

Key target regressions from the issue/spec:
- old-version compatibility paths (`py27`, `py35`, `py36`, `py37`)
- `PersonClass` recognition / validator matching
- `pymempool_objects` undercounting
- `deque` off-by-one on `py38`
- `class-merge-py27` dict recognition / merge behavior

The end state must also pass:
- `tests/test_issue_120_python_testdata_regression.py`

## Instructions

- Must follow:
  - `.symphony_prompt.md`
  - `dev-flow/test-cases.md`
  - `dev-flow/plan.md`
- Must validate via the real regression chain:
  - `python3 testdata/run_test.py <case>`
  - do **not** bypass using direct `validate.py`
- Acceptance requirements:
  - all 16 runnable Python testdata cases pass sequentially
  - representative versions `py27`, `py311`, `py312` pass
  - no new Python regressions
  - root cause + fix result recorded in `dev-log/`
- Required git workflow at the end:
  - commit changes
  - commit message format: `feat: <description>`
  - include `Resolves #120` in commit body
- Must **not** commit:
  - `dev-flow/plan.md`
  - `dev-flow/test-cases.md`
  - `dev-flow/*-dev-report.md`
  - `dev-flow/*-qa-report.md`
- Must write a timestamped dev report in `dev-flow/<timestamp>-dev-report.md` before finishing, but do not commit it.
- Keep diff minimal and focused; no unnecessary dependencies.


- all 16 runnable Python testdata cases pass sequentially
- representative versions `py27`, `py311`, `py312` pass
